ZZZ_dummy_forpol_category = {
	ZZZ_USA_HAI_Blitz_Combat_Stagnates = { # May evaluate, Haiti is priority and Blitz seems to be fine
		allowed = { original_tag = ZZZ }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		priority = 20

		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					HAI = {
						has_war_with = DOM
					}
				}
			}
		}
		selectable_mission = no
		days_mission_timeout = 28
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout ZZZ_USA_HAI_Blitz_Combat_Stagnates"
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								NOT = {
									has_game_rule = {
										rule = TRUJILLO_BLITZ_OUTCOME
										option = TRUJILLO_BLITZ_OUTCOME_CASEFIRE_HAI
									}
								}
								DOM = {
									controls_province = 15584
									controls_province = 15636
								}
							}
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = TRUJILLO_BLITZ_OUTCOME
								option = TRUJILLO_BLITZ_OUTCOME_CASEFIRE_DOM
							}
						}
					}
					USA = { TNO_HIS_blitz_ceasefire_trujillo = yes }
				}
				else =	{
					USA = { TNO_HIS_blitz_ceasefire_haiti = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Landing Missions
	ZZZ_PPI_Invasion_Ends = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_border_war
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_puerto_plata_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = PPI_landing_ongoing
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_global_flag = PPI_ceasefire_happening
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { country_exists = CAL }
			}
		}

		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 62

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				# conclusion events moved to victory scripted effects
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout ZZZ_PPI_Invasion_Ends"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_PP_collapse_tooltip
			USA = {
				hidden_effect = {
					log = "war_won"
					if = { # Balaguer coup -> Ceasefire
						limit = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									CAL = {
										controls_state = 1237 # Puerto Plata
										OR = {
											controls_state = 1709 # Cibao Norte
											controls_state = 1708 # Duarte
										}
									}
									NOT = {
										has_game_rule = {
											rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
											option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_DOM_VICTORY
										}
									}
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
									option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_REV_VICTORY
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
									option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_BAL_VICTORY
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
									option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_BAL_CEASEFIRE
								}
							}
						}

						DOM = { save_global_event_target_as = losing_country }
						CAL = { save_global_event_target_as = winning_country }
						set_global_flag = war_won
						set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
						add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }

						TNO_PPI_DOM_ceasefire = yes
					}
					else = { # Invasion collapses
						CAL = { save_global_event_target_as = losing_country }
						DOM = { save_global_event_target_as = winning_country }
						set_global_flag = war_won
						set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
						add_to_variable = { global.peace_popup_dirty = 1 }

						TNO_PPI_DOM_victory_trujillo = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				subtract_from_variable = { UPH.UPH_unsung_warriors_speed = 0.04 }
				subtract_from_variable = { UPH.UPH_unsung_warriors_breakthrough = 0.06 }
				subtract_from_variable = { SPH.SPH_para_sa_ating_himagsikan_attack = 0.04 }
				subtract_from_variable = { SPH.SPH_para_sa_ating_himagsikan_speed = 0.04 }
				subtract_from_variable = { SPH.SPH_para_sa_ating_himagsikan_breakthrough = 0.06 }
				add_to_variable = { USA.USA_UPH_Morale_Drops = 1 }
				hidden_effect = {
					ZZZ = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { USA.USA_UPH_Morale_Drops < 5 }
							}
							activate_mission = ZZZ_USA_Philippines_Dummy

USA_proxy_war_homefront_GUI = {
	USA_SAW_increase_manpower_timer = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		days_mission_timeout = 70
		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 1

		priority = 100

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = yes
					USA = { has_war = yes }
				}
			}
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = no
						has_country_flag = USA_homefront_mech_active
					}
					AND = {
						USA = { has_war = no }
						has_country_flag = USA_homefront_mech_active
					}
				}
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_SAW_increase_manpower_timer"
			USA_service_manpower_pulse_positive = yes
		}
	}
	USA_SAW_decrease_manpower_timer = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat_red
		days_mission_timeout = 70
		is_good = no

		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 1

		priority = 100

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = no
					USA = { has_war = no }
				}
			}
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						USA_homefront_has_active_proxy = yes
						has_country_flag = USA_homefront_mech_active
					}
					AND = {
						USA = { has_war = yes }
						has_country_flag = USA_homefront_mech_active
					}
				}
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_SAW_decrease_manpower_timer"
			USA_service_manpower_pulse_negative = yes
		}
	}

	USA_WAC_discontent_declines = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat_red
		allowed = {
			always = no
			original_tag = USA
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 7
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent = 0 }
				tooltip = USA_WAC_discontent_is_gone_tt
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision complete USA_WAC_discontent_declines"
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout USA_WAC_discontent_declines"
			USA_WAC_discontent_decrease = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 0 } }
					activate_mission = USA_WAC_discontent_declines
				}
				else = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_WAC_discontent }
					clear_variable = WAC_discontent_stability
					clear_variable = WAC_discontent_war_support
					clear_variable = WAC_discontent_political_power
				}
			}

		}
	}

	############ WAW MISSIONS PORT OVER ############
		## CAPITULATION ##
	USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_use_force
		priority = 2000

		days_mission_timeout = 35
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no

		available = {
			CAO = { controls_state = 793 }
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = { # Success
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates_success_tt
			set_temp_variable = { tempTrust = 15 }
			USA_change_trust_in_government = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_global_flag = west_african_war_ongoing
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAO }
					leave_faction = yes
					every_enemy_country = { white_peace = PREV }
				}
				CAO = { dismantle_faction = yes }

				if = { # Scenario 1
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1 }

					ZZZ = {
						WAC_1_WAA_VICTORY = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { country_exists = YOR }
						every_country = {
							limit = { has_war_with = YOR }
							white_peace = YOR
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { # Scenario 2
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_2 }

					FFR = {
						save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
					}
					ZZZ = {
						WAC_2_PALF_BEATEN = yes
					}
				}
				else = { # Scenario 3
					if = {
						limit = { country_exists = YOR }
						every_country = {
							limit = { has_war_with = YOR }
							white_peace = YOR
						}
					}
					ZZZ = {
						WAC_3_FMA_VICTORY = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_effect = { # Failure
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission complete USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_cameroon_capitulates_failure_tt
			USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
		}
	}

	## WAR DECISIONS ##
	USA_WAC_stabilize_front = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat
		priority = 101
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_frontlines_selected = yes
			NOT = { has_global_flag = WAC_fronts_stabilized }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3 }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 50
		days_remove = 7
		is_good = yes

		fire_only_once = yes

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAC_stabilize_front_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = WAC_fronts_stabilized
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = { global.west_african_nations = THIS }
						has_war = yes
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = WEST_AFRICA_idea_chaotic_front
						add_idea = WEST_AFRICA_idea_stable_front
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	### GARRISON AND DISCONTENT MISSIONS ###

	USA_WAC_garrisons_weaken = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock_red
		priority = 1000

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no

		fire_only_once = no

		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_garrisons_weaken"
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.WAC_escalation
						value = 15
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -2 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 15 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -4 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 25 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -6 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 50 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -10 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 70 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -12 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = USA_WAC_garrisons_weaken
			}
		}
	}

	USA_WAC_discontent_rises = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock_red
		priority = 1000

		days_mission_timeout = 90
		is_good = no
		selectable_mission = no

		fire_only_once = no

		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR
		}

		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: mission timeout USA_WAC_discontent_rises"
			hidden_effect = { # war crimes event. Only fire once
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 75 }
					}
					country_event = { id = west_african_crisis.50 days = 14 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 50 }
					}
					country_event = { id = west_african_crisis.49 days = 14 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_wac_garrison_strength > 80 }
				}
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_small = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_wac_garrison_strength > 60 }
				}
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_medium = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_wac_garrison_strength > 40 }
				}
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
			}
			else = {
				USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 10 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -6 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 30 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -8 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 50 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -10 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_WAC_WAR_Discontent > 70 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -12 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
			}
			else = {
				USA_decrease_optics_small = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { USA_optics > 80 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_government = liberalism
							has_government = conservatism
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_all_voters_header_tt
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_pro = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_pro_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_pro }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_pro_shift

					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_nat = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_minority_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_nativists_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_urban_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_rural_nat_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_nat }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_nat_shift

					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_foreign_policy_con = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_union_foreign_policy_con_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_foreign_policy_con }
					add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_black_foreign_policy_con_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_foreign_policy_con }
					add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_hispanic_foreign_policy_con_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_foreign_policy_con }
					add_to_variable = { Policy_Shift_minority_foreign_policy_con_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_foreign_policy_con }

					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_foreign_policy_con

				}
				if = {

						OR = {
							has_government = progressivism
							has_government = paternalism
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_all_voters_header_tt
					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_dem = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_union_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_dem }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_black_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_dem }
					add_to_variable = { Demographic_Shift_hispanic_dem_Weeks = USA_week_change_union_dem }

					set_temp_variable = { USA_week_change_union_rep = 1 }

					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_union_foreign_policy_con
				}

			if = {

					check_variable = {
						var = global.WAC_escalation
						value = 20

					}
				}
				USA_WAC_discontent_increase_v_small = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 20 }

				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 30 }
				}
				USA_WAC_discontent_increase = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 40 }
				}
				USA_WAC_discontent_increase_large = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { global.WAC_escalation > 50 }
				}
				USA_WAC_discontent_increase_v_large = yes
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = USA_WAC_discontent_rises
			}
		}
	}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {

	TNO_jamaica_guerrilla_attack = {
		priority = 10
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_jamaica_crisis_guerrillas
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_crisis_guerrillas_done
			clr_country_flag = USA_jamaica_crisis_guerrillas
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_intensify_OFN_propaganda = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		cost = 10

		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_low = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_low = yes
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_discourse
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
			#WIN = { check_variable = { WIN_foreign_intervention > 40 } }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { GDP > 0 } }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_50_million

		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders_cost
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { removed_from_reserves = money_reserves }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = removed_from_reserves min = 0 max = 0.05 }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = removed_from_reserves }
				add_to_variable = { national_debt = to_add_to_debt }
			}
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_blackmail_independence_activists = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_document_cancel
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
			#WIN = { check_variable = { WIN_foreign_intervention > 75 } }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_us_intervention > 75 }
			}
		}

		days_remove = 21
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
			TNO_increase_us_intervention_high = yes
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_foreign_intervention_medium_us = yes

			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum_trigger
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed < 3 }
			}
			TNO_US_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}
		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = no

		cost = 15

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed > 0 }
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_postpone_referendum_effect

			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 0 } }
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening }
				} else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WIN.WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 1 } }
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening_2 }
				} else = {
				WIN = { set_country_flag = TNO_WIN_delay_happening_3 }
			}


			hidden_effect = {
				WIN = {
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_days_left = 7 }
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_days_max = 7 }
					add_to_variable = { WIN_referendum_times_delayed = 1 }


					# Recompute clock
					set_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = 100 }
					multiply_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = WIN_referendum_days_left }
					divide_variable = { WIN_referendum_fill = WIN_referendum_days_max }
				}

			}
		}
	}


	TNO_jamaica_investigate_interference = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_investigate
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes

			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { TNO_foreign_intervention_high_us = yes }

					TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes

			}
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_dial_back_rhetoric = {

					}

			}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {

	USA_OC_increase_commitment = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		visible = {
			tag = USA
			TNO_fopo_baathism_support_selected = yes
			TNO_volunteer_cap_less_5 = yes
			check_variable = {
				USA_OC_volunteer_sent < 3
			}
			#is supporting at least one country
			set_temp_variable = { war_counter = 0 }
			any_country = {
				is_in_array = { global.OIL_supported_by_USA = THIS }
				has_war = yes
			}
		}

		cost = 50
		days_re_enable = 21

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_OC_increase_commitment"
			add_command_power = 25

			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.OIL_supported_by_USA

				USA = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = PREV }
					TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
				}
			}

			add_to_variable = {
				USA_OC_volunteer_sent = 1
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = OIL_USA_increase_volunteers_1


			add_to_variable = {
				USA_OC_participation = 8
				tooltip = BOR_OC_add_participation
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_OC_participation min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

			factor = 150
		}

			add_to_temp_variable = { tempEscalation = 10 }

					type = infrastructure
					damage = 1
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_INS_bombings = 1 }
			FROM = {

					static_modifiers = { targeted_bombing_campaign }
					province = { all_provinces = yes }

			}
		}

			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check = 15 }
			check_variable = {
				var = command_power
				value = t_cp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = political_power
				value = t_pp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_pp_dynamic

					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}
				send_equipment = {
					equipment = infantry_equipment
					amount = 1000
					target = INS
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { FRI = { has_capitulated = no } }
					send_equipment = {
						equipment = infantry_equipment
						amount = 150
						target = FRI
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { DMP = { has_capitulated = no } }

						equipment = infantry_equipment
						amount = 150
						target = DMP
					}

				if = {

					send_equipment = {
						equipment = infantry_equipment
						amount = 150
						target = NII
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { DMS = { has_capitulated = no } }
					send_equipment = {
						equipment = infantry_equipment
						amount = 150
						target = DMS
					}
				}
				if = {

						target = ABD

			INS_ICW_change_escalation = yes
			add_to_array = { USA_bombing_array = 795 }
			add_to_array = { USA_bombing_array = 1753 }
			add_to_array = { USA_bombing_array = 797 }
			add_to_array = { USA_bombing_array = 1557 }
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_authorize_operation_linebacker_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}
				for_each_loop = {
					array = USA_bombing_array
					if = { #I LOVE LONG BRACKET CHAINS FOR SIMPLE CODE
						limit = {
							var:USA_bombing_array^i = {
								NOT = {
									is_fully_controlled_by = INS
								}
							}
						}
						var:USA_bombing_array^i = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 5
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				for_each_loop = {
					array = USA_bombing_array
					if = { #I LOVE LONG BRACKET CHAINS FOR SIMPLE CODE
						limit = {
							var:USA_bombing_array^i = {
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										is_fully_controlled_by = FRI
										is_fully_controlled_by = DMP
										is_fully_controlled_by = NII
										is_fully_controlled_by = DMS
										is_fully_controlled_by = ABD
										is_fully_controlled_by = PMT
										is_fully_controlled_by = SLS
									}
								}
							}
						}
						var:USA_bombing_array^i = {
							damage_building = {
								type = infrastructure
								damage = 5
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clear_array = USA_bombing_array
		}
	}

			TNO_fopo_saw_frontlines_selected = yes
			has_country_flag = SAW_large_shipments_enabled
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 29.99
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp_30_pp

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		targets = { AST BRA CAN NZL SAF }
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = SAF
					SAF = { has_volunteers_amount_from = { tag = PREV count > 0 } }
				}
			}
		}

		days_remove = 30
		days_re_enable = 30
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 add_political_power = -30 }
			set_country_flag = SAW_active_shipment
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = SAW_active_shipment
			send_equipment = {
				type = motorized_equipment_2
				amount = 500
				target = FROM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "No Step Back"
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = MBT_chassis_2
					amount = 250
					target = FROM
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = IFV_chassis_2
					amount = 200
					target = FROM
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = APC_chassis_2
					amount = 300
					target = FROM
				}
			}
			else = {
				send_equipment = {
					type = MBT_equipment_2
					amount = 250
					target = FROM
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = IFV_equipment_2
					amount = 200
					target = FROM
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = APC_equipment_2
					amount = 300
					target = FROM
				}
			}
			USA_increase_trust_in_government_small = yes
		}
	}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {
	USA_meeting_with_generals_mozambique = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_handshake
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mozambique_selected = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		cost = 100
		days_re_enable = 120
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_meeting_with_generals"
			add_command_power = 40
		}

	}

	USA_bombing_runs_mozambique = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mozambique_selected = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 120
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 14.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 90

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_bombing_runs"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = US_aid_mozambique_simango }
				if = { #Check for whether Simango was supported and 2 countries need to be hit
					limit = { country_exists = GAZ } #Don't hit annexed countries
					GAZ = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
							days = 90
						}
						TNO_worsen_poverty_high = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { country_exists = GZO }
					GZO = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
							days = 90
						}
						TNO_worsen_poverty_high = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				GAZ = {
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
						days = 90
					}
					TNO_worsen_poverty_high = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_sabotage_effort_mozambique = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mozambique_selected = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 90
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 24.99
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp_25_pp

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_sabotage_effort"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
				add_political_power = -25
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = US_aid_mozambique_simango }
				if = { #Check for whether Simango was supported and 2 countries need to be hit
					limit = { country_exists = GAZ } #Don't hit annexed countries
					GAZ = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_sabotage_effort
							days = 90
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { country_exists = GZO }
					GZO = {
						add_timed_idea = {
							idea = USA_sabotage_effort
							days = 90
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				GAZ = {
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = USA_sabotage_effort
						days = 90
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_the_african_quagmire = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_hat_skull
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Mandates_East_Africa_Decolonized
						has_country_flag = Mandates_Angola_Decolonized
						has_country_flag = Mandates_Central_Africa_Decolonized
					}
				}
			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 60
		is_good = yes ###after all, you want'd to stay in and spread the good of the free world... right?

		fire_only_once = no

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Pulled_Out }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { USA_mandates_cost = 0.5 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_mandates_cost max = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mandates_cost_tt
			set_temp_variable = { tempHawkishness = -1.5 }
			USA_change_hawkishness = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_mandate_protest_fired } }
				set_country_flag = USA_mandate_protest_fired
				USA_africa_shared_discontent_fire_effect = yes
			}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_variable = USA_withdraw_cost_trust } }
				set_variable = { USA_withdraw_cost_trust = -10 }
				set_variable = { USA_withdraw_pp = 300 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_withdraw_cost_available
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { USA_withdraw_cost_trust < -5 } }
				add_to_variable = { USA_withdraw_cost_trust = 1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { USA_withdraw_pp = 15 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_withdraw_cost_tt
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							NOT = {
								has_global_flag = CAR_FORMED
								has_country_flag = Mandates_Angola_collapsed
							}
							check_variable = { ANG.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = {
								has_global_flag = CAR_FORMED
								has_country_flag = Mandates_East_Africa_collapsed
							}
							check_variable = { MZB.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
						AND = {
							NOT = {
								has_global_flag = CAR_FORMED
								has_country_flag = Mandates_Central_Africa_collapsed
							}
							check_variable = { COG.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
						AND = {
							has_global_flag = CAR_FORMED
							check_variable = { USC.OFN_MANDATE_rebel_stability < 0.5 }
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mandates_low_stability_warning_tt
				set_temp_variable = { tempOptics = -5 }
				USA_change_optics = yes
				set_temp_variable = { tempTrust = -5 }
				USA_change_trust_in_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	USA_distribute_PADESM_leaflets = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_document_concessions
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_madagascar_selected = yes
			TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_fopo_Madagascar_Contribution_Above_30 = yes
			check_variable = { MADCW_limited_actions > -1 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		cost = 20
		days_re_enable = 120

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_distribute_PADESM_leaflets"

			set_temp_variable = { us_side_swap = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { germoney_side_swap = -2 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { us_side_swap = US_opp_strength_mad }
			multiply_temp_variable = { germoney_side_swap = US_opp_strength_mad }

			var:Madagascar_selected_city = {
				add_to_variable = { Madagascar_strength_var_USA = us_side_swap }
				add_to_variable = { Madagascar_strength_var_GER = germoney_side_swap }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = Madagascar_strength_var_USA
					min = 0
					max = 100
				}
				set_variable = { Madagascar_strength_var_JAP = Madagascar_strength_var_USA }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = Madagascar_strength_var_GER
					min = 0
					max = 100
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { us_side_swap = 2 } }
				custom_effect_tooltip = MADCW_increases_strength_in_state_by_2_tt
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = MADCW_increases_strength_in_state_by_4_tt
			}

			set_temp_variable = { TEMP_MADCW_Factionalism = 10 }
			MAD_adjust_USA_factionalism = yes

			USA_operation_less = yes
			# increases state control
			# increases US factionalism
			# increases US investment
			# increases US contribution
		}

	}

				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Isolated_Authority }

					division = "name = \"Fizarana Infantry\" division_template = \"Fizarana Infantry\" start_experience_factor = 0.5"
					owner = MAD
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
				}

			}

		}

		}

		custom_cost_text = MAD_CW_CCT_Faction

			}

		}

	USA_ai_state_shift = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ofn_stationing
		available = { #
			NOT = { country_exists = MDG }
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 2
		timeout_effect = { # dumbest fucking work around possible; im not coding AI logic.
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 1969.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 100
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
						TNO_fopo_MDM_controls_state = yes
						check_variable = { 1969.Madagascar_strength_var_USA > 39 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000
						1969 = { has_state_flag = MAD_CW_USAI_FOCUS }
					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 1969 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 945.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000
						944 = { has_state_flag = MAD_CW_USAI_FOCUS }
					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 944 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						check_variable = { 945.Madagascar_strength_var_USA > 10 }
						check_variable = { 945.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000
						945 = { has_state_flag = MAD_CW_USAI_FOCUS }
					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 945 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 1970.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 100
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
						TNO_fopo_MDM_controls_state = yes
						check_variable = { 1970.Madagascar_strength_var_USA > 39 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000
						1970 = { has_state_flag = MAD_CW_USAI_FOCUS }
					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 1970 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 1974.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 100
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
						TNO_fopo_MDM_controls_state = yes
						check_variable = { 1974.Madagascar_strength_var_USA > 39 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000
						1974 = { has_state_flag = MAD_CW_USAI_FOCUS }
					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 1974 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 1975.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 100
						TNO_fopo_MADCW_War_Stage_1 = yes

						check_variable = { 1975.Madagascar_strength_var_USA > 39 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000

					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 1975 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 1860.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1000
						1860 = { has_state_flag = MAD_CW_USAI_FOCUS }
					}
					set_variable = { Madagascar_selected_city = 1860 }
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						NOT = { check_variable = { 946.Madagascar_strength_var_USA < 60 } }
					}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {

	USA_mano_timer = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			has_global_flag = mano_campaign_over
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}
		priority = 200
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 100
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission timeout USA_mano_timer"
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mano_success_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = west_african_crisis.19
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	USA_mano_deploy_taskforce = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_aircraft_carrier
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			has_global_flag = mano_campaign_ongoing
			TNO_mano_have_enough_ships = yes
		}
		priority = 95
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 21

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission complete USA_mano_deploy_taskforce"
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = -14
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_mano_air_operation
			set_country_flag = USA_mano_allow_air
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission timeout USA_mano_deploy_taskforce"
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = 14
			}
			USA_decrease_trust_in_government_large = yes
		}
	}

	USA_mano_brazilian_logistics = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_supply
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
			is_in_faction_with = BRA
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		cost = 10
		complete_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = -7
			}
		}
	}

	USA_mano_intensify_mobilization = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
		}
		cost = 25
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete intensify_mobilization"
			USA_increase_service_manpower_depletion_rate_small = yes
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = -7
			}
		}
	}

	USA_mano_increase_troop_allocation = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
			check_variable = { mano_volunteer_count < 2 }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 14.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp

		days_remove = 3
		days_re_enable = 10

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete increase_troop_allocation"
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = -7
			}
			USA_increase_service_manpower_depletion_rate_large = yes
			add_to_variable = { mano_volunteer_count = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -15
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove increase_troop_allocation"
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = LIB
				}
				set_temp_variable = { target = LIB }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add = 1 }
				TNO_add_num_volunteers = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = MDI
				}
				set_temp_variable = { target = MDI }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add = 1 }
				TNO_add_num_volunteers = yes
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = -7
			}
		}
	}

	USA_mano_focus_resource = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				OR = {
					LIB = { has_idea = LIB_idea_usa_resource }
					MDI = { has_idea = LIB_idea_usa_resource }
				}
			}
		}
		cost = 20

		days_re_enable = 30

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_emergency_weapons"
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = LIB
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 350
					target = LIB
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 50
					target = LIB
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = anti_tank_equipment
					amount = 50
					target = LIB
				}
				LIB = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_idea = LIB_idea_usa_resource }
						}
						add_ideas = LIB_idea_usa_resource
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = MDI
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 350
					target = MDI
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 50
					target = MDI
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = anti_tank_equipment
					amount = 50
					target = MDI
				}
				MDI = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_idea = LIB_idea_usa_resource }
						}
						add_ideas = LIB_idea_usa_resource
					}
				}
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}

	USA_mano_divert_resource_to_air = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_mano_allow_air
			TNO_mano_have_enough_ships = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 14.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 30

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_bombing_runs_mano"
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = LIB }
				proxy_war_clear_dynamic_bombing = yes
			}
			add_fuel = -5000
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = USA_mano_timer
				days = 14
			}
		}
	}

	USA_mano_frontline_bombing = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			has_country_flag = USA_mano_allow_air
			TNO_mano_have_enough_ships = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 14.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 30

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 }
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_bombing_runs_mano"
			USA_decrease_optics_medium = yes
			USA_increase_trust_in_government_small = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAO }

				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = USA_Plane_Bombing
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			fuel_cost = 200
		}
	}

	USA_mano_scorched_earth = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_mano_campaign_selected = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 90
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 24.99
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp_25_pp

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_sabotage_effort"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
				add_political_power = -25
			}
			USA_decrease_optics_medium = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = LIB
						is_owned_by = MDI
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = Mano_state_scorched_earth_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

##		 Puerto Plata Invasion       ##
#######################################
USA_foreign_policy_category = {
	## Debug ##
	USA_PPI_hidden = {
		priority = 14990
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_civil_support
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_puerto_plata_selected = yes
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = PPI_proxy_war_preparation
				has_global_flag = PPI_landing_ongoing
				ZZZ = { has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_DOM_CAL_Negotiations }
			}
			ZZZ = {
				OR = {
					has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_Invasion_Begins
					has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_CAL_training
					has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_Invasion_Ends
					has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_DOM_CAL_Negotiations
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			always = no
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_PPI_hidden"
			effect_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { ZZZ = { has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_Invasion_Begins } }

				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { ZZZ = { has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_CAL_training } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_PPI_CAL_training_tt
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { ZZZ = { has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_Invasion_Ends } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_PP_collapse_tooltip
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { ZZZ = { has_active_mission = ZZZ_PPI_DOM_CAL_Negotiations } }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_PP_negotiations_tooltip
				}
			}
		}
	}

	## Invasion Preparation ##
	USA_PPI_Prepare_USN_Landing_Support = {
		#ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_phone_call
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_puerto_plata_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = PPI_proxy_war_preparation
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check = 15 }
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check_extra = t_cp_check }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { t_cp_check_extra = 0.01 }

			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check = 30 }
			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check_extra = t_pp_check }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { t_pp_check_extra = 0.01 }

			command_power > t_cp_check_extra
			has_political_power > t_pp_check_extra
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_pp_dynamic

		fire_only_once = yes
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_PPI_Prepare_USN_Landing_Support"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -15 add_political_power = -30 }

			set_country_flag = USA_PPI_USN_support
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_PPI_USN_support_tt
		}
	}
	USA_PPI_Authorize_Air_Support = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_PPI_USAF_support_tt
		}
	}

	USA_PPI_Organize_Supplies = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_supply_indent
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_puerto_plata_selected = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_show_supply_decisions
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = PPI_landing_ongoing
				has_global_flag = PPI_proxy_war_preparation
			}
			is_ai = no
		}

		days_remove = 7
		#days_re_enable = 14

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check = MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_cp }
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check_extra = t_cp_check }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { t_cp_check_extra = 0.01 }

			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check = MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_pp }
			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check_extra = t_cp_check }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { t_pp_check_extra = 0.01 }

			command_power > t_cp_check_extra
			has_political_power > t_pp_check_extra
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_pp_dynamic

		remove_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_cp = 4 }
				add_to_variable = { MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_pp = 8 }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { MEX.pp_supply_decision_effect > 5 } }
					subtract_from_variable = { MEX.pp_supply_decision_effect = 1 }
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_PPI_Organize_Supplies"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_cp add_political_power = -MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_pp }
			set_temp_variable = { invasion_supply_temp = MEX.pp_supply_decision_effect }
			TNO_USA_PP_invasion_supply_add = yes
		}
	}
	USA_PPI_Organize_Supplies_AI = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_action_indent
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_political_power < -200
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { USA.US_PP_supply_perc < USA.US_PP_supply }
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_puerto_plata_selected = yes
			has_country_flag = USA_show_supply_decisions
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = PPI_landing_ongoing
				has_global_flag = PPI_proxy_war_preparation
			}
			is_ai = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 10

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_PPI_Organize_Supplies_AI"
			add_to_variable = { MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_cp = 4 }
			add_to_variable = { MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_pp = 8 }
			set_temp_variable = { invasion_supply_temp = 10 }
			TNO_USA_PP_invasion_supply_add = yes

			set_temp_variable = { USA_PPI_supply_cp = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { USA_PPI_supply_pp = -1 }

			multiply_temp_variable = { USA_PPI_supply_cp = MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_cp }
			add_political_power = USA_PPI_supply_cp

			multiply_temp_variable = { USA_PPI_supply_pp = MEX.pp_supply_decision_cost_pp }
			add_command_power = USA_PPI_supply_pp
		}
	}

			command_power > t_cp_check_extra
			has_political_power > t_pp_check_extra
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_pp_dynamic

		days_remove = 30
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision USA_PPI_Recruitment_Campaign"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 add_political_power = -20 }

			set_temp_variable = { spy_strength_temp = 4 }
			TNO_PP_spy_strength_decrease_USA = yes
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_war_with = DOM }
				add_manpower = 2000
			}
			set_temp_variable = { invasion_supply_temp = 3 }
			TNO_USA_PP_invasion_supply_add = yes
			set_temp_variable = { insurgency_strength_temp = 5 }
			TNO_PP_insurgency_strength_increase = yes
		}
	}

				IBR = { remove_mission = IBR_PPI_tensions_increase remove_mission = IBR_PPI_ceasefire_ends }
				GER = { remove_mission = GER_PPI_tensions_increase remove_mission = GER_PPI_ceasefire_ends }
			}
		}
	}
	USA_PPI_tensions_increase = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_revolt
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_puerto_plata_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = PPI_ceasefire_happening
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_global_flag = PPI_ceasefire_successful
		}
		available = {
			has_global_flag = PPI_ceasefire_collapsed
		}

		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7

		timeout_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { ceasefire_tension_temp = 5 }
			TNO_PPI_increase_ceasefire_tension = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = USA_PPI_tensions_increase
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME
							option = PUERTO_PLATA_INVANSION_OUTCOME_BAL_CEASEFIRE
						}
						has_country_flag = USA_PP_ceasefire_balaguer
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						CCP_PPI_time_checker = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								CCP_PPI_time_checker = 5
							}
							is_ai = yes
						}
						set_country_flag = TNO_PPI_open_negotiations
						add_political_power = -35
						IBR = {
							country_event = {
								id = HIS_PP_ceasefire.4
								days = 2
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								CCP_PPI_time_checker = 9
							}
							is_ai = yes
						}
						add_political_power = -40
						TNO_PPI_DOM_negotiated_peace = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

USA_foreign_policy_category = {
	USA_WAFR_reconstruction_timeout = {
		allowed = { original_tag = USA }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wafr_reconstruction_selected = yes
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 240
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					check_variable = { WAF_average_reconstruction > 80 }
				}
				WAF_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { WAF_average_reconstruction > 89 } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAFR_reconstruction_success_tt
				WAF_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = USA_WAFR_reconstruction_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = free_france_reconstruction.6 }
				TNO_fopo_remove_wafr_reconstruction_tab = yes
				set_global_flag = FFR_reconstruction_failed
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = free_france_reconstruction.13 days = 32 }
			}

			clear_variable = USA_WAFR_urban_development_state
			clear_variable = USA_WAFR_naval_base_state
			clear_variable = USA_WAFR_corporate_interactions_tracker

		}
	}
